def extract_mirp_features(mirp):
    rates = [p_data.rate for p_data in mirp.ports.values()]
    feature_vec = rates
    return feature_vec

n_ports = 9
n_vcs = 4
n_periods = 30
seed = 1
n_instances = 1000

n = 50
test_range = range(50)

lp_dir = '.'

base_folder = '%s/ports%d_vcs%d_t%d_seed%d_n%d' % (lp_dir,
                                                   n_ports,
                                                   n_vcs,
                                                   n_periods,
                                                   seed,
                                                   n_instances)

instance_files = ['%s/instance_i%d_data.txt' % (base_folder, i)
                  for i in test_range]

# EXTRACT ROUTES
print("[ Extracting Routes ]")
instance_rates = {}
for i in test_range:
    instance_file = instance_files[i]
    mirp = generator.load(instance_file)
    instance_rates[i] = np.array(extract_mirp_features(mirp))

    
dist = np.zeros((n,n))
for i in range(n):
    for j in range(n):
        dist[i,j] = np.linalg.norm(instance_rates[i]-instance_rates[j])

plt.figure()
plt.imshow(dist)

[ Extracting Routes ]

In [18]:
def preprocess(n, data, normalize=True):
    matrix = np.zeros((n,n))
    gap = [data['baseline'][i] - data['relax_col_gen'][i]
           for i in range(n)]
    
    for i,j in itertools.product(range(n), range(n)):
        matrix[i,j] = data['baseline'][i] - data['seeded'][i][j]['ip_obj']
    
    if normalize:
        for i,j in itertools.product(range(n), range(n)):
            matrix[i,j] = matrix[i,j] / gap[i]
    
    return matrix

def process(n, data):
    matrix = np.zeros((n,n))
    relaxgap = [data['baseline'][i] - data['relax_col_gen'][i]
           for i in range(n)]
    
    ipgap = [data['baseline'][i] - data['original_ip'][i]
             for i in range(n)]
    
    plt.figure(figsize=(5,5))
    plt.hist(relaxgap)
    plt.title('Histogram of ColGen IP minus Relaxation')
    
    plt.figure(figsize=(5,5))
    plt.hist(ipgap)
    plt.title('Histogram of ColGen IP minus Original IP')
    
    for i,j in itertools.product(range(n), range(n)):
        matrix[i,j] = data['baseline'][i] - data['seeded'][i][j]['ip_obj']
    
    matrix_relax_normed = np.zeros((n,n))
    matrix_ip_normed = np.zeros((n,n))
    for i,j in itertools.product(range(n), range(n)):
        matrix_relax_normed[i,j] = matrix[i,j] / relaxgap[i]
        matrix_ip_normed[i,j] = matrix[i,j] / ipgap[i]
        
    matrix_ip_normed = matrix_relax_normed
    
    plt.figure(figsize=(15,12))
    plt.subplot(221)
    plt.imshow(dist)
    
    plt.figure(figsize=(20,5))
    plt.subplot(131)
    sns.heatmap(matrix, linewidth=0)
    plt.subplot(132)
    #plt.imshow(matrix_relax_normed)
    sns.heatmap(matrix_relax_normed, linewidth=0)
    plt.subplot(133)
    sns.heatmap(matrix_ip_normed, linewidth=0)
    #plt.imshow(matrix_ip_normed)
    
    M = matrix_ip_normed
    dist2 = np.copy(dist)
    indices = dist2 < 0.01
    dist2[indices] = 0.01
    M = np.divide(np.ones(dist2.shape),dist2)
    order = get_order(M) 
    print(order)
    M = np.copy(dist)
    plt.figure(figsize=(5,5))
    M = M[:,order]
    M = M[order,:]
    plt.imshow(M)
    M = np.copy(matrix_ip_normed)
    plt.figure(figsize=(5,5))
    M = M[:,order]
    M = M[order,:]
    plt.imshow(M)
    
    plt.figure(figsize=(15,10))
    threshold_loc_pairs = [(0,231), (0.1,232), (0.2,233), (0.3,234), (0.4,235)]     
    for threshold, loc in threshold_loc_pairs:
        nu_matrix = np.copy(matrix_ip_normed)
        indices = nu_matrix > threshold
        other_indices = nu_matrix <= threshold
        nu_matrix[indices] = 1
        nu_matrix[other_indices] = 0
        M = nu_matrix
        #M = np.ones(M.shape) - M
        #order = get_order(M)
        #M = M[:,order]
        #M = M[order,:]
        plt.subplot(loc)
        plt.title('Threshold: %.1f' % threshold)
        plt.imshow(M)
        #plt.savefig('nu_%d.png' % threshold, bbox_inches='tight')
        #sns.heatmap(nu_matrix, linewidth=0.5)
        
    plt.figure(figsize=(15,5))
    plt.subplot(131)
    plt.hist(matrix_ip_normed[30,:])
    plt.subplot(132)
    plt.hist(matrix_ip_normed[8,:])
    plt.subplot(133)
    plt.hist(matrix_ip_normed[47,:])
    
    for i in [30,8,47]:
        print(data['baseline'][i])
        print(data['original_ip'][i])
    
def process_multi(n, datasets):
    matrices = []
    for data in datasets:
        matrix = preprocess(n, data)
        matrices.append(matrix)

    plt.figure(figsize=(15,5))
    loc = 130
    for matrix in matrices:
        loc += 1
        plt.subplot(loc)
        plt.imshow(matrix)
    
    plt.figure(figsize=(15,10))
    loc = 230
    for threshold in [0, 3000]:
        for matrix in matrices:
            loc += 1
            nu_matrix = np.copy(matrix)
            indices = nu_matrix > threshold
            other_indices = nu_matrix <= threshold
            nu_matrix[indices] = 1
            nu_matrix[other_indices] = 0
            plt.subplot(loc)
            plt.title('Threshold: %.1f' % threshold)
            plt.imshow(nu_matrix)
        #plt.savefig('nu_%d.png' % threshold, bbox_inches='tight')
        #sns.heatmap(nu_matrix, linewidth=0.5)

    #plt.imshow(matrix, cmap='hot')
In [19]:
def laplacian(M):
    n = M.shape[0]
    A = M + M.transpose()
    Lap_A = np.diag(np.dot(A,np.ones(n))) - A
    return Lap_A

def get_order(M):
    L_A = laplacian(M)
    w, v = np.linalg.eig(L_A)
    fiedler = v[:,1]
    return np.argsort(fiedler)

n = 50
with open(pickle_file, 'rb') as f:
    data = pickle.load(f)

seeded_data = data['seeded']

for instance_idx in range(n):
    instance_data = seeded_data[instance_idx]
    print("Processing Instance %d ..." % instance_idx)
    print("- true ip obj: %.2f" % (data['original_ip'][instance_idx]))
    print("- baseline ip obj: %.2f" % (data['baseline'][instance_idx]))
    print("- column gen relax obj: %.2f" % (data['relax_col_gen'][instance_idx]))
    # ip diff is with respect to baseline, positive is good
    for i in range(n):
        combo_data = instance_data[i]
        print("    (%d,%d) -- rounds: %d, routes: %d, relax: %.2f, ip diff: %.2f, percent gap closed: %.2f"
              % (instance_idx, i,
                 combo_data['rounds'],
                 combo_data['n_routes'],
                 combo_data['relax_obj'],
                 data['baseline'][instance_idx] - combo_data['ip_obj'],
                 100*(data['baseline'][instance_idx] - combo_data['ip_obj'])/(data['baseline'][instance_idx] - data['original_ip'][instance_idx])))
    print("")
